### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.1.5
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.5 on Github, visit [v24.1.5 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.5).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.3-261-gf629e9a3a88...v24.1.5](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.3-261-gf629e9a3a88...v24.1.5)

### General changes

- Upgraded the `grpc` version to v1.56.3. [#130046](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130046)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Introduced the new [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `changefeed.protect_timestamp.lag`, which controls when a [changefeed's](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) protected timestamp is updated. The [protected timestamp](/docs/v24.1/architecture/storage-layer#protected-timestamps) will only be updated if the set `changefeed.protect_timestamp.lag` value has passed between the last protected timestamp and the [changefeed high watermark](/docs/v24.1/how-does-an-enterprise-changefeed-work). [#129686](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129686)
- [`SHOW CHANGEFEED JOB`](/docs/v24.1/show-jobs#show-changefeed-jobs), `SHOW CHANGEFEED JOBS`, and [`SHOW JOBS`](/docs/v24.1/show-jobs) no longer expose user-sensitive information like `client_key`. [#122636](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122636)
- Added two network metrics, `changefeed.network.bytes_in` and `changefeed.network.bytes_out`. These metrics track the number of bytes sent by individual [changefeeds](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) to the following sinks:
    - [Kafka sinks](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks#kafka). If [child metrics](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled) are enabled, the metric will have a `kafka` label.
    - [Webhook sinks](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks#webhook-sink). If [child metrics](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled) are enabled, the metric will have a `webhook` label.
    - [Pub/Sub sinks](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks#google-cloud-pub-sub). If [child metrics](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled) are enabled, the metric will have a `pubsub` label.
    - [SQL sink](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-for). If [child metrics](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-server-child-metrics-enabled) are enabled, the metric will have a `sql` label. [#130584](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130584)

### SQL language changes

- The session setting [`plan_cache_mode=force_generic_plan`](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) can now be used to force [prepared statements](/docs/v24.1/savepoint#savepoints-and-prepared-statements) to use query plans that are [optimized](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) once, and reused in future executions without re-optimization, as long as it does not become stale due to [schema changes](/docs/v24.1/online-schema-changes) or a collection of new [table statistics](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics). The setting takes effect during `EXECUTE` commands. [`EXPLAIN ANALYZE`](/docs/v24.1/explain-analyze) includes a `plan type` field. If a generic query plan is optimized for the current execution, the `plan type` will be `generic, re-optimized`. If a generic query plan is reused for the current execution without performing optimization, the `plan type` will be `generic, reused`. Otherwise, the `plan type` will be `custom`. [#128085](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128085)
- The session setting [`plan_cache_mode=auto`](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) can now be used to instruct the system to automatically determine whether to use `custom` or `generic` query plans for the execution of a [prepared statement](/docs/v24.1/savepoint#savepoints-and-prepared-statements). Custom query plans are optimized on every execution, while generic plans are [optimized](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) once and reused on future executions as-is. Generic query plans are beneficial in cases where query optimization contributes significant overhead to the total cost of executing a query. [#128085](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128085)

### Operational changes

- There are now structured [logging events](/docs/v24.1/logging) that report connection breakage during node shutdown. Previously, the logs existed, but were unstructured. The logs appear in the [`OPS` logging channel](/docs/v24.1/logging#ops). There are two new events:
    - The `node_shutdown_connection_timeout` event is logged after the timeout defined by the [`server.shutdown.connections.timeout`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) cluster setting transpires, if there are still open SQL connections.
    - The `node_shutdown_transaction_timeout` event is logged after the timeout defined by the [`server.shutdown.transactions.timeout`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) cluster setting transpires, if there are still open transactions on those SQL connections. [#128711](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128711)
- Added a new configuration parameter `server.cidr_mapping_url`, which maps IPv4 CIDR blocks to arbitrary tag names. [#130051](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130051)
- Modified the metrics `sql.bytesin` and `sql.bytesout` to work as aggregate metrics if [child metrics](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) are enabled. [#130051](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130051)
- Added three new network-tracking metrics. `rpc.connection.connected` is the number of rRPC TCP level connections established to remote nodes. `rpc.client.bytes.egress` is the number of TCP bytes sent via gRPC on connections CockroachDB initiates. `rpc.client.bytes.ingress` is the number of TCP bytes received via gRPC on connections CockroachDB initiated. [#130050](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130050)
- This commit adds two metrics: `changefeed.network.bytes_in` and `changefeed.network.bytes_out`. These metrics track the number of bytes sent by the individual [changefeeds](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) to different [sinks](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks). [#130584](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130584)

### DB Console changes

- The user experience for [metrics](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview-dashboard) charges in the [DB Console](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview) now has hover behavior that focuses on individual lines and shows values under the mouse pointer. [#128867](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128867)
- Users with the [`VIEWACTIVITY`](/docs/v24.1/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges) privilege can download statement bundles from the [DB Console](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview). [#129503](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129503)
- Users with the [`VIEWACTIVITY`](/docs/v24.1/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges) privilege can now request, view, and cancel statement bundles in the [DB Console](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview). [#129805](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129805)
- The [DB Console](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview) will show a notification alerting customers without an Enterprise license to [upcoming license changes](https://www.cockroachlabs.com/enterprise-license-update) with a link to more information. [#130510](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130510)

### Bug fixes

- Previously, [declarative](/docs/v24.1/online-schema-changes) and legacy [schema changes](/docs/v24.1/online-schema-changes) were incorrectly allowed to be run concurrently, which could lead to failing or hung schema change jobs. [#128805](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128805)
- Fixed a bug that caused errors like `ERROR: column 'crdb_internal_idx_expr' does not exist` when accessing a table with an [expression index](/docs/v24.1/expression-indexes) where the expression evaluates to an `ENUM` type, for example, `CREATE INDEX ON t ((col::an_enum))`. [#129093](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129093)
- Fixed a bug where `NaN` or `Inf` could not be used as the default value for a parameter in [`CREATE FUNCTION`](/docs/v24.1/create-function) statements. [#129086](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129086)
- Fixed a bug in which [`SELECT... FOR UPDATE` and `SELECT... FOR SHARE`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update) queries using [`SKIP LOCKED`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update#wait-policies) and a [`LIMIT` and/or an `OFFSET`](/docs/v24.1/limit-offset) could return incorrect results under [`READ COMMITTED`](/docs/v24.1/read-committed) isolation. This bug was present when support for `SKIP LOCKED` under `READ COMMITTED` isolation was introduced in v24.1.0. [#128101](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128101)
- Fixed a bug in which some [`SELECT... FOR UPDATE` or `SELECT... FOR SHARE`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update) queries using [`SKIP LOCKED`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update#wait-policies) could still block on locked rows when using [`optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable`](/docs/v24.1/session-variables#optimizer-use-lock-op-for-serializable) under [`SERIALIZABLE`](/docs/v24.1/demo-serializable) isolation. This bug was present when `optimizer_use_lock_op_for_serializable` was introduced in v24.1.0. [#128101](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128101)
- Function input parameters for [user-defined functions](/docs/v24.1/user-defined-functions) can no longer be of the `VOID` type, which matches the behavior of PostgreSQL. [#129280](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129280)
- Fixed a bug in the public preview of [Write Ahead Log (WAL) Failover](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start#write-ahead-log-wal-failover) that could prevent a node from starting if it crashed during a failover. [#129367](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129367)
- [Starting nodes](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start) could fail with: `could not insert session...: unexpected value`, if an ambiguous result error was encountered when inserting into the `sqlliveness` table. [#129234](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129234)
- Internally issued queries that are not initiated within a [SQL session](/docs/v24.1/show-sessions) no longer respect a [statement timeout](/docs/v24.1/session-variables#statement-timeout). This includes: background [jobs](/docs/v24.1/show-jobs), queries issued by the [DB Console](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview) that perform introspection, and the [Cloud SQL shell](/docs/cockroachcloud/sql-shell). [#129515](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129515)
- Fixed a rare bug in [`SHOW CLUSTER SETTING`](/docs/v24.1/show-cluster-setting) that could cause it to fail with an error like `timed out: value differs between local setting and KV`. [#129756](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129756)
- Fixed a bug where the [`schema_locked` table parameter](/docs/v24.1/with-storage-parameter#table-parameters) did not prevent a table from being referenced by a [foreign key](/docs/v24.1/foreign-key). [#129754](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129754)
- Fixed a bug where the [`require_explicit_primary_keys` session variable](/docs/v24.1/session-variables#require-explicit-primary-keys) would aggressively prevent all [`CREATE TABLE`](/docs/v24.1/create-table) statements from working. [#129907](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/129907)
- Fixed a slow-building memory leak when using [Kerberos authentication](/docs/v24.1/gssapi_authentication). [#130318](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130318)
- Fixed a potential memory leak in [changefeeds](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) using a [cloud storage sink](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks#cloud-storage-sink). The memory leak could occur if both the cluster settings [`changefeed.fast_gzip.enabled`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-changefeed-fast-gzip-enabled) and [`changefeed.cloudstorage.async_flush.enabled`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) are set to `true` and the changefeed received an error while attempting to write to the cloud storage sink. [#130626](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130626)
- Fixed a bug that prevented buffered file sinks from being included when iterating over all file sinks. This led to problems such as the `debug zip` command not being able to fetch logs for a cluster where buffering was enabled. [#130158](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/130158)

## v24.1.4

Release Date: August 29, 2024

### Downloads

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.1.4
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.4 on Github, visit [v24.1.4 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.4).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.3...v24.1.4](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.3...v24.1.4)

### Security updates

- URLs in the following SQL statements are now sanitized of any secrets before being written to [unredacted logs](/docs/v24.1/configure-logs#redact-logs). [#127506](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127506)
    - [`ALTER BACKUP SCHEDULE`](/docs/v24.1/alter-backup-schedule)
    - [`ALTER BACKUP`](/docs/v24.1/alter-backup)
    - [`ALTER CHANGEFEED SET sink`](/docs/v24.1/alter-changefeed#set-options-on-a-changefeed)
    - [`BACKUP`](/docs/v24.1/backup)
    - [`COPY`](/docs/v24.1/copy)
    - [`CREATE CHANGEFEED`](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed)
    - [`CREATE EXTERNAL CONNECTION`](/docs/v24.1/create-external-connection)
    - [`CREATE SCHEDULE FOR BACKUP`](/docs/v24.1/create-schedule-for-backup)
    - [`CREATE SCHEDULE FOR CHANGEFEED`](/docs/v24.1/create-schedule-for-changefeed)
    - [`EXPORT`](/docs/v24.1/export)
    - [`IMPORT INTO`](/docs/v24.1/import-into)
    - [`RESTORE`](/docs/v24.1/restore)
    - [`SHOW BACKUPS`](/docs/v24.1/show-backup)
    - [`SHOW BACKUP`](/docs/v24.1/show-backup)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added a new Kafka [changefeed sink](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks) that uses the [`franz-go` library](https://github.com/twmb/franz-go) and CockroachDB's `batching_sink` implementation. The new Kafka sink can be enabled with the `changefeed.new_kafka_sink_enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings), which is disabled by default. [#128018](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128018)
- The new Kafka sink, enabled with [`changefeed.new_kafka_sink_enabled`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings), as well as the Google Cloud Pub/Sub sink, now display notices indicating the topics that a changefeed will emit to. [#128333](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128333)

### SQL language changes

- Added a new `sql.auth.grant_option_for_owner.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) to prevent the [`GRANT OPTION`](/docs/v24.1/show-grants#privilege-grants) from being given to the owner of an object by default. The cluster setting defaults to `true`, retaining the existing behavior; when it is set to `false`, the `GRANT OPTION` is not implicitly given to an object's owner. The owner will still have all privileges on an object except the ability to grant privileges to other users. [#126959](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126959)

### Command-line changes

- A `--locality-file` flag is now available on the [`cockroach start`](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start) and [`cockroach start-single-node`](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start-single-node) commands. This allows specifying node [locality](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start#locality) (typically a `region` value) as a file, rather than by using the [`--locality` flag](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start#locality). [#127475](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127475)

### DB Console changes

- The [**Databases** and **Tables** pages](/docs/v24.1/ui-databases-page) in the DB Console now show a loading state while loading information for databases and tables, including size and range counts. [#127748](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127748)
- On the [**Databases** page](/docs/v24.1/ui-databases-page) in the DB Console, table names will no longer appear with quotes around the schema and table name. [#127766](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127766)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2.0 in which CockroachDB would hit an internal error when evaluating [`INSERT`s](/docs/v24.1/insert) into [`REGIONAL BY ROW`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#set-the-table-locality-to-regional-by-row) tables where the source was a [`VALUES`](/docs/v24.1/selection-queries#values-clause) clause with a single row and at least one Boolean expression. [#127277](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127277)
- Fixed a bug in which the [`DISCARD`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table) statement was disallowed when the [session setting](/docs/v24.1/session-variables#default-transaction-read-only) `default_transaction_read_only` was set to `on`. [#127363](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127363)
- In the [DB Console event log](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview-dashboard#events-panel), [`ALTER ROLE`](/docs/v24.1/alter-role) events now display correctly even when no [role options](/docs/v24.1/alter-role#role-options) are included in the `ALTER ROLE` statement. [#126568](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126568)
- Fixed a formatting issue with the `sql_sequence_cached_node` value of the [`serial_normalization` session setting](/docs/v24.1/session-variables). This could lead to an error connecting to CockroachDB if this value was set as the default for `serial_normalization` via the cluster setting [`sql.defaults.serial_normalization`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-sql-defaults-serial-normalization). [#127673](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127673)
- Fixed a bug where [dropping `ENUM` values](/docs/v24.1/alter-type#drop-a-value-in-a-user-defined-type) that were referenced by [index expressions](/docs/v24.1/expression-indexes) could fail with an error. [#127454](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127454)
- Fixed a bug that caused a memory leak when executing SQL statements with [comments](/docs/v24.1/comment-on), for example, `SELECT /* comment */ 1;`. Memory owned by a SQL session would continue to grow as these types of statements were executed. The memory would only be released when closing the [SQL session](/docs/v24.1/show-sessions). This bug had been present since v23.1. [#127759](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127759)
- Fixed a bug where [schema changes](/docs/v24.1/online-schema-changes) could hang if the lease rangefeed stopped receiving updates. [#127487](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127487)
- Fixed small memory leaks that would occur during [changefeed](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) creation. [#128018](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128018)
- Fixed a memory leak that could occur when specifying a non-existent [virtual cluster](/docs/v24.1/cluster-virtualization-overview) name in the connection string. [#128106](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128106)
- Fixed a bug where [`CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS`](/docs/v24.1/create-index) would not correctly short-circuit if the given index already existed. [#128311](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128311)
- Fixed a bug in syntax validation, in which the `DESCENDING` clause was not allowed for non-terminal columns of an [inverted index](/docs/v24.1/inverted-indexes). Only the last column of an inverted index should be prevented from being `DESCENDING`. This is now properly checked. [#128311](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128311)
- Fixed a bug where an [index](/docs/v24.1/indexes) could store a column in the primary index if that column had a mixed-case name. [#128311](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128311)
- Setting or dropping a default value on a [computed column](/docs/v24.1/computed-columns) is now blocked, even for `NULL` defaults. Previously, setting or dropping a default value on a computed column was a no-op. [#128466](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128466)
- Fixed a bug that could cause spurious user permission errors when multiple databases shared a common schema with a routine referencing a table. The bug had existed since v22.2 when [user-defined functions (UDFs)](/docs/v24.1/user-defined-functions) were introduced. [#126412](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126412)
- Fixed a bug where [`debug zip`](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-debug-zip) would return an error while fetching unstructured/malformed logs. [#128605](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128605)
- Fixed a bug where a hash-sharded [constraint](/docs/v24.1/constraints) could not be created if it referred to columns that had a backslash in the name. [#128521](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128521)
- Fixed a bug in which the output of [`EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT)`](/docs/v24.1/explain) for various `CREATE` statements was not redacted. This bug had existed since [`EXPLAIN (REDACT)`](/docs/v24.1/explain#parameters) was introduced in v23.1 and affects the following statements:
    - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE TABLE`
    - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE VIEW`
    - `EXPLAIN (OPT, REDACT) CREATE FUNCTION` [#128489](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/128489)

## v24.1.3

Release Date: August 1, 2024

### Downloads

<Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.1.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.3 on Github, visit [v24.1.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.2...v24.1.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.2...v24.1.3)

### SQL language changes

- [`EXPLAIN ANALYZE`](/docs/v23.2/explain-analyze) statements are now supported when executed via Cloud Console [SQL shell](/docs/cockroachcloud/sql-shell). [#125563](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125563)
- Added the [`sql.auth.grant_option_inheritance.enabled` cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-sql-auth-grant-option-inheritance-enabled). The default value is `true`, which maintains consistency with CockroachDB's previous behavior: users granted a privilege with [`WITH GRANT OPTION`](/docs/v24.1/grant) can in turn grant that privilege to others. When `sql.auth.grant_option_inheritance.enabled` is set to `false`, the `GRANT OPTION` is not inherited through role membership, thereby preventing descendant roles from granting the privilege to others. However, the privilege itself continues to be inherited through role membership. [#126300](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126300)

### Operational changes

- `crdb_internal.cluster_execution_insights.txt` and `crdb_internal.cluster_txn_execution_insights.txt` have been removed from the [debug zip](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-debug-zip). These files contained cluster-wide insights for statements and transactions. Users can still rely on the [per-node execution](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-debug-zip#files) insights in `crdb_internal.node_execution_insights.txt` and `crdb_internal.node_txn_execution_insights.txt`. [#125807](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125807)
- For the [TELEMETRY logging channel](/docs/v24.1/logging#telemetry), TCL `sampled_query` events will now be sampled at the rate specified by the setting [`sql.telemetry.query_sampling.max_event_frequency`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-sql-telemetry-query-sampling-max-event-frequency), which is already used to limit the rate of sampling DML statements. [#126729](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126729)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where collection of [debug information](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-debug-zip) for very long-running [jobs](/docs/v24.1/show-jobs) could use excessive space in the `job_info` system table and cause some interactions with the jobs system to become slow. [#126122](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126122)
- Fixed a bug where a change to a [user-defined type (UDT)](/docs/v24.1/create-type) could cause queries against tables using that type to fail with an error: `histogram.go:694: span must be fully contained in the bucket`. The change to the user-defined type could come directly from an [`ALTER TYPE`](/docs/v24.1/alter-type) statement, or indirectly from an [`ALTER DATABASE ADD REGION`](/docs/v24.1/alter-database#add-region) or [`DROP REGION`](/docs/v24.1/alter-database#drop-region) statement (which implicitly change the [`crdb_internal_region`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#set-the-table-locality-to-regional-by-row) type). This bug has existed since UDTs were introduced in v20.2. [#125800](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125800)
- Fixed a bug in which constant [`LIKE`](/docs/v24.1/sql-feature-support#scalar-expressions-and-boolean-formulas) patterns containing certain sequences of backslashes did not become constrained scans. This bug has been present since v21.1.13 when support for building constrained scans from `LIKE` patterns containing backslashes was added. [#125539](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125539)
- Fixed the statistics estimation code in the [optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) so it does not use the empty histograms produced if [histogram collection](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer#control-histogram-collection) has been disabled during stats collection due to excessive memory utilization. Now the optimizer will rely on distinct counts instead of the empty histograms and should produce better plans as a result. This bug has existed since CockroachDB v22.1. [#126153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126153)
- Fixed a bug where [`CREATE TABLE`](/docs/v24.1/create-table) statements with [index expressions](/docs/v24.1/expression-indexes) could hit undefined column errors on [transaction retries](/docs/v24.1/transactions#transaction-retries). [#125967](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125967)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB would hit an internal error when evaluating [`INSERT`s](/docs/v24.1/insert) into [`REGIONAL BY ROW`](/docs/v24.1/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables) tables where the source is a [`VALUES` clause](/docs/v24.1/selection-queries#values-clause) with a single row and at least one boolean expression. The bug was introduced in v23.2.0. [#125505](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125505)
- Fixed a bug in [`cockroach debug tsdump`](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-debug-tsdump) where the command fails when a custom SQL port is used and the [`--format=raw`](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-debug-tsdump#flags) flag is provided. [#125980](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125980)
- Fixed a bug where a [user-defined function (UDF)](/docs/v24.1/user-defined-functions) that shared a name with a [built-in function](/docs/v24.1/functions-and-operators#built-in-functions) would not be resolved, even if the UDF had higher precedence according to the [`search_path`](/docs/v24.1/sql-name-resolution#search-path) variable. [#126296](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126296)
- Fixed a bug that caused [background jobs](/docs/v24.1/show-jobs) to incorrectly respect a statement timeout. [#126820](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126820)
- Fixed a bug where [`ALTER DATABASE... DROP REGION`](/docs/v24.1/alter-database#drop-region) could fail if any tables under the given database have [indexes on expressions](/docs/v24.1/expression-indexes). [#126599](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126599)
- Fixed a PostgreSQL incompatibility bug when inputting `public` as user name for [built-in functions](/docs/v24.1/functions-and-operators) such as `has_database_privilege` and `has_schema_privilege`. [#126851](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126851)
- Fixed a bug when [restoring](/docs/v24.1/restore) a database with a [composite type](/docs/v24.1/create-type#create-a-composite-data-type). [#126428](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126428)
- Fixed a bug where the [Databases](/docs/v24.1/ui-databases-page) page crashed if the range information was not available. [#127092](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127092)
- Fixed a bug where CockroachDB could incorrectly evaluate an [`IS NOT NULL`](/docs/v24.1/null-handling#nulls-and-simple-comparisons) filter if it was applied to non- `NULL` tuples that had `NULL` elements, such as `(1, NULL)` or `(NULL, NULL)`. This bug has existed since v20.2. [#126938](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126938)
- The `sql_sequence_cached_node` value of the [`serial_normalization` setting](/docs/v24.1/serial#modes-of-operation) was not correctly formatted. This could lead to errors while connecting to CockroachDB if the default value of `serial_normalization` was set to `serial_normalization`. The formatting bug was fixed, which also fixes the errors when connecting. [#127675](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/127675)

### Performance improvements

- Starting a `cockroach` process will no longer flush buffered [logs](/docs/v24.1/logging-overview) to configured [logging sinks](/docs/v24.1/configure-logs#configure-log-sinks) unless the process is running under `systemd`, where cockroach runs with the `NOTIFY_SOCKET` environment variable. [#126305](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126305)
- [Schema changes](/docs/v24.1/online-schema-changes) that cause a data backfill, such as adding a non-nullable column or changing the primary key, will now split and scatter the temporary indexes used to perform the change. This reduces the chance of causing a [write hotspot](/docs/v24.1/performance-best-practices-overview#hot-spots) that can slow down foreground traffic. [#126684](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126684)

### Contributors

This release includes 122 merged PRs by 39 authors.

## v24.1.2

Release Date: July 2, 2024

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.1.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.2 on Github, visit [v24.1.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.1...v24.1.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.1...v24.1.2)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added error messages for unsupported Apache Pulsar [changefeed](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed) sink parameters, e.g. `topic_prefix is not yet supported`. [#124666](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124666)
- Fixed a bug that was present since v22.2 where [changefeeds](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) with long-running [initial scans](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed#initial-scan) might incorrectly restore checkpoint job progress and drop events during [changefeed restarts](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-messages#duplicate-messages) due to transient errors or node restarts. The bug was most likely to occur in clusters with the following contributing factors:
    - The `changefeed.shutdown_checkpoint.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) was enabled.
    - The cluster settings `changefeed.frontier_checkpoint_frequency` and `low changefeed.frontier_highwater_lag_checkpoint_threshold` were set low, which resulted in the initial scan taking many multiples of the configured frequency to complete.
    - There were multiple target tables with significant differences in row counts in one changefeed.
    - The changefeed target tables were large with many ranges.
    - The initial scan took a long time to complete (an hour or longer). [#124996](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124996)

### Operational changes

- Improved [disk usage metric reporting](/docs/v24.1/ui-cluster-overview-page#capacity-metrics) over volumes that dynamically change their size over the life of the `cockroach` process. [#125050](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125050)
- The default values for the following [cluster settings](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) were updated from `100000` to `7500`. These settings control the maximum number of [fingerprints](/docs/v24.1/ui-statements-page#sql-statement-fingerprints) (distinct combinations of statements and [transactions](/docs/v24.1/transactions) ) CockroachDB can store in memory, with stats being flushed on a `10m` [interval](/docs/v24.1/interval) by default. You can increase these settings if your workload produces more unique fingerprints than this amount within the flush interval, and you notice that SQL stats are missing. [cockroachdb/cockroach#125554](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125554)
    - [`sql.metrics.max_mem_stmt_fingerprints`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-sql-metrics-max-mem-stmt-fingerprints)
    - [`sql.metrics.max_mem_txn_fingerprints`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-sql-metrics-max-mem-txn-fingerprints)

### DB Console changes

- The favicon now renders properly for [DB Console](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview), along with other image files. [#122706](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122706)

### Bug fixes

- [`SHOW TYPES`](/docs/v24.1/show-types) now includes [user-defined composite types](/docs/v24.1/create-type#create-a-composite-data-type). It had omitted those types ever since composite types were added in v23.1. [#124817](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124817)
- Fixed a crash introduced in v24.1.0-beta.2 that could occur when planning [statistics](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics) collection on a table with a [virtual computed column](/docs/v24.1/computed-columns) using a [user-defined type](/docs/v24.1/create-type) when the [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-sql-stats-virtual-computed-columns-enabled) `sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled` (introduced in v24.1.0-alpha.1) was set to `true`. [#124996](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124996)
- Fixed handling in the [declarative schema changer](/docs/v24.1/online-schema-changes) when columns are included in the `STORING()` clause of a [`CREATE INDEX`](/docs/v24.1/create-index) statement. CockroachDB now checks if the column is virtual up-front, and properly detects when a column is already handled by an existing [`INDEX`](/docs/v24.1/indexes) when the column name has UTF-8 characters. [#125153](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125153)
- Fixed a bug where a change to a [user-defined type](/docs/v24.1/create-type) could cause queries against tables using that type to fail with an error message like: `"histogram.go:694: span must be fully contained in the bucket"`. The change to the user-defined type could come directly from an [`ALTER TYPE`](/docs/v24.1/alter-type) statement, or indirectly from an [`ALTER DATABASE... ADD REGION`](/docs/v24.1/alter-database#add-region) or [`DROP REGION`](/docs/v24.1/alter-database#drop-region) statement (which implicitly changes the `crdb_internal_region` type). This bug had existed since UDTs were introduced in v20.2. [#124810](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124810)
- Fixed a bug where [telemetry logs](/docs/v24.1/logging#telemetry) had the same [statement fingerprint](/docs/v24.1/ui-statements-page#sql-statement-fingerprints) ID for different SQL statements. [#125000](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125000)
- Fixed an issue where [adding a column](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#add-column) with a default value of an empty [array](/docs/v24.1/array) would not succeed. [#125325](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125325)
- [`ALTER TABLE... ADD CONSTRAINT UNIQUE`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table) will now fail with a well-formed error message and code `42601` if a statement tries to add a [unique constraint](/docs/v24.1/unique) on an expression. [#125417](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125417)
- Fixed a bug where the [`public` schema](/docs/v24.1/schema-design-overview#schemas) would be created with the wrong owner. Previously the [`admin` role](/docs/v24.1/security-reference/authorization#roles) would own the `public` schema. Now, the database owner is also the owner of the `public` schema. The owner can be altered after the schema is created. [#125533](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125533)
- Fixed a bug in v24.1, v23.2, and v23.1 where using the `changefeed.aggregator.flush_jitter` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings#setting-changefeed-aggregator-flush-jitter) with the [`min_checkpoint_frequency`](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed#min-checkpoint-frequency) option set to `0` could cause panics. [#125459](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125459)
- The log message `"expiration of liveness record... is not greater than expiration of the previous lease... after liveness heartbeat"` is no longer generated. [#125449](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125449)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2.0 in which CockroachDB would hit an internal error when evaluating [`INSERT`s](/docs/v24.1/insert) into [`REGIONAL BY ROW`](/docs/v24.1/table-localities#regional-by-row-tables) tables where the source was a `VALUES` clause with a single row and at least one boolean expression. [#126209](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/126209)

### Performance improvements

- Improved the efficiency of error handling in the [vectorized execution engine](/docs/v24.1/vectorized-execution) to reduce the CPU overhead of statement timeout handling and reduce the potential for more statement timeouts. [#124996](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124996)
- Some [privilege](/docs/v24.1/security-reference/authorization#managing-privileges) checks when scanning the `crdb_internal.system_jobs` internal table now happen once before the scan, instead of once for each row. This improves performance for queries that read from `crdb_internal.system_jobs`. [#125250](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/125250)

### Miscellaneous

- A [changefeed](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed) optimization to reduce duplicates during aggregator restarts has been disabled due to poor performance. [#124996](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124996)

### Contributors

This release includes 78 merged PRs by 35 authors.

## v24.1.1

Release Date: June 14, 2024

### Downloads

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.1.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.1 on Github, visit [v24.1.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0...v24.1.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0...v24.1.1)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2 where a [changefeed](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) with a long-running [initial scan](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed#initial-scan) might incorrectly restore checkpoint job progress and drop events during a [changefeed restart](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-messages#duplicate-messages) due to transient errors or node restarts. The bug was most likely to occur in clusters with the following contributing factors:
    - The `changefeed.shutdown_checkpoint.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) was enabled (in clusters running v23.2 and later).
    - The cluster settings `changefeed.frontier_checkpoint_frequency` and `low changefeed.frontier_highwater_lag_checkpoint_threshold` were set low, which resulted in the initial scan taking many multiples of the configured frequency to complete.
    - There were multiple target tables with significant differences in row counts in one changefeed.
    - The changefeed target tables were large with many ranges.
    - The initial scan took a long time to complete (an hour or longer). [#123967](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123967)
- History retention jobs created upon completion of [cluster replication](/docs/v24.1/physical-cluster-replication-overview) no longer erroneously indicate that they failed when they expire. [#124055](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124055)

### SQL language changes

- The [optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) can now plan constrained scans over partial indexes in more cases, particularly on partial indexes with predicates referencing [virtual computed columns](/docs/v24.1/computed-columns#virtual-computed-columns). [#123468](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123468)
- The storage parameter `ttl_delete_rate_limit`, which determines the rate limit for deleting expired rows, is now set to `100` by default. [#124354](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124354)
- CockroachDB no longer limits precision when converting [spatial data types](/docs/v24.1/architecture/glossary#data-types) to JSON. [#124536](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124536)
- The `optimizer_push_offset_into_index_join` [session setting](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) has been added. When enabled, the [optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) will attempt to push offset expressions into index join expressions to produce more efficient query plans. The setting is enabled by default on v24.1 and later, and disabled on v23.2. [#124490](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124490)
- The default value of the `sql.defaults.results_buffer.size` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) has been changed from 16KiB to 512KiB. This reduces the chance that clients using [`READ COMMITTED`](/docs/v24.1/read-committed) transactions will encounter errors that cannot automatically be retried within CockroachDB. [#124633](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124633)

### Operational changes

- The default values for the [cluster settings](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `sql.metrics.max_mem_stmt_fingerprints` and `sql.metrics.max_mem_txn_fingerprints` have been changed from `100000` to `5000`, thus lowering the default limits for in-memory statement and transaction fingerprints. [#123430](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123430)
- The new `sql.pgwire.pipeline.count` [gauge metric](/docs/v24.1/metrics) shows the number of wire protocol commands that have been received by the server, but have not yet begun processing. This metric will only grow if clients are using the "pipeline mode" of the PostgreSQL wire protocol. [#124256](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124256)
- The `client_authentication_ok` and `client_session_end` messages are now logged to the `SESSIONS` [log channel](/docs/v24.1/logging-overview#logging-channels) unconditionally. Previously, these would be logged only if the `server.auth_log.sql_sessions.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) was set to `true`. All other `SESSIONS` log messages are logged only if `server.auth_log.sql_sessions.enabled` or `server.auth_log.sql_connections.enabled` are set to `true`. To prevent logging of `client_authentication_ok` or `client_session_end` messages, you can optionally disable the `SESSIONS` log channel. [#124369](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124369)

### DB Console changes

- Fixed a bug where the [replication lag metric](/docs/v24.1/physical-cluster-replication-monitoring) would falsely report high lag for multi-node clusters and on cutover. [#123585](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123585)
- Fixed a bug that caused [**SQL Activity**](/docs/v23.2/ui-sql-dashboard) entries sorted by `% of Runtime` to be sorted incorrectly. [#123903](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123903)
- The "Admission Delay Rate", "Admission Work Rate", and "Requests Waiting For Flow Tokens" time-series charts have been removed from the DB Console. These charts can be difficult to interpret and provide little value for overload investigations. [#124509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124509)
- The [**Overload** dashboard](/docs/v24.1/ui-overload-dashboard) now includes descriptions for all metrics. [#124509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124509)
- Metrics on the [**Overload** dashboard](/docs/v24.1/ui-overload-dashboard) have been reordered to improve their categorization. The metrics are now roughly in the following order: 1. Metrics to help determine which resource is constrained (IO, CPU); 2. Metrics to narrow down which [admission control](/docs/v24.1/admission-control) queues are seeing requests waiting; 3. More advanced metrics about system health (goroutine scheduler, L0 sublevels, etc.). [#124509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124509)
- New metrics `cr.store.storage.l0-sublevels` and `cr.node.go.scheduler_latency-p99.9` on the [**Overload** dashboard](/docs/v24.1/ui-overload-dashboard) provide better visibility into overloaded resources. [#124509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124509)
- There are now four separate graphs for Admission Queue Delay: 1. Foreground (regular) CPU work; 2. Store (IO) work; 3. Background (elastic) CPU work; 4. Replication Admission Control (store overload on replicas). [#124509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124509)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that would occur when [`ALTER TYPE... DROP VALUE`](/docs/v24.1/alter-type) is followed by `DROP SCHEMA CASCADE...` in the same transaction. Previously, the `ALTER TYPE` schema change would get queued up to run at commit time, but by that point, the type may have already been removed, so the commit could fail. [#123577](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123577)
- Tables are now automatically repaired when the errors `invalid inbound foreign key... origin table ID should be...` or `invalid outbound foreign key... reference table ID should be...` occur. [#123668](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123668)
- Fixed a bug where a failed [`RESTORE`](/docs/v24.1/restore) could not be retried without manual intervention. [#123205](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123205)
- Fixed a bug introduced in alpha versions of v23.1 where calling a routine could result in an unexpected `function... does not exist` error. The bug is triggered when the routine is called twice using the exact same SQL query, and either: (a) the routine has polymorphic arguments, or: (b) between the two calls, the routine is replaced by a routine with the same name and different parameters. [#123516](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123516)
- Fixed a rare bug where a lease transfer could lead to a `side-transport update saw closed timestamp regression` panic. The bug could occur when a node was overloaded and [failing to heartbeat its node liveness record](/docs/v24.1/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#node-liveness-issues). [#123533](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123533)
- Fixed a crash introduced in v24.1.0-beta.2 that could occur when planning statistics collection on a table with a [virtual computed column](/docs/v24.1/computed-columns#virtual-computed-columns) using a [user-defined type](/docs/v24.1/create-type) when the newly-introduced [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled` is set to `true`. (The setting was introduced in v24.1.0-alpha.1, and defaults to `true`.) [#124060](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124060)
- Fixed a bug where an [`ALTER TABLE... ALTER PRIMARY KEY`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#alter-primary-key) statement could hang if the table had any indexes that were referred to by [views](/docs/v24.1/views) or [functions](/docs/v24.1/functions-and-operators) using the `FORCE INDEX` clause. [#124323](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124323)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v24.1.0 where the `max_decimal_digits` argument of the `st_geojson` [builtin function](/docs/v24.1/functions-and-operators#built-in-functions) was ignored and the default was used instead. [#124502](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124502)
- Scattering a range with a replication factor of 1 now no longer erroneously up-replicates the range to two replicas. Leases will also no longer thrash between nodes when perturbed with a replication factor of 1. [#124453](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124453)
- Fixed a bug where, if the `ttl_row_stats_poll_interval` storage parameter was non-zero for a table with [row-level TTL](/docs/v24.1/row-level-ttl) enabled, the queries issued to update row statistics could block the job from completing. Now, if the job completes, these statistics queries are cancelled. This means that the `jobs.row_level_ttl.total_rows` and `jobs.row_level_ttl.total_expired_rows` metrics will report `0` if the job finishes before the row stats queries complete. [#124627](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124627)
- Fixed a bug where a [`DROP ROLE`](/docs/v24.1/drop-role) or [`DROP USER`](/docs/v24.1/drop-user) command could leave references behind inside types, which could prevent subsequent [`SHOW GRANTS`](/docs/v24.1/show-grants) commands from working. [#124619](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124619)
- Fixed a bug where the `results_buffer_size` [session variable](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) could not be configured by using the "options" query parameter in the connection string, but only as a top-level query parameter. Now, `results_buffer_size` can be configured in either part of the connection string. This variable still cannot be changed with the [`SET`](/docs/v24.1/set-vars) command after the session begins. [#124775](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124775)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v20.2 where a change to a [user-defined type](/docs/v24.1/create-type) could cause queries against tables using that type to fail with an error message like `histogram.go:694: span must be fully contained in the bucket`. The change to the user-defined type could come directly from an [`ALTER TYPE`](/docs/v24.1/alter-type) statement, or indirectly from an [`ALTER DATABASE... ADD REGION`](/docs/v24.1/alter-database#add-region) or [`DROP REGION`](/docs/v24.1/alter-database#drop-region) statement (which implicitly change the `crdb_internal_region` type). [#124856](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124856)

### Performance improvements

- Improved the efficiency of error handling in the [vectorized execution engine](/docs/v24.1/vectorized-execution) in order to reduce the CPU overhead of statement timeout handling and reduce the potential for more statement timeouts. [#123499](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123499)
- Due to its poor performance, a [changefeed](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) optimization that aimed to reduce duplicates during aggregator restarts due to its bad performance has been disabled. [#123595](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123595)

### Contributors

This release includes 173 merged PRs by 42 authors.

## v24.1.0

Release Date: May 20, 2024

With the release of CockroachDB v24.1, we've added new capabilities to help you migrate, build, and operate more efficiently. Refer to our summary of the most significant user-facing changes under [Feature Highlights](#v24-1-0-feature-highlights).

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach:v24.1.0
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0 on Github, visit [v24.1.0 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0).

#### Performance

<table><thead><tr><th class="center-align" colspan="1" rowspan="2">Feature</th><th class="center-align" colspan="4" rowspan="1">Availability</th></tr><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Ver.</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Self-Hosted</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Dedicated</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Serverless</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>WAL (Write-Ahead Logging) Failover<br/><br/>When a CockroachDB node is configured to run with multiple stores, you can mitigate some effects of disk stalls by configuring the node to <a href="/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start#write-ahead-log-wal-failover">failover the store's write-ahead log (WAL)</a> to another store's data directory.<br/><br/>This feature is in preview.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Autocommit DDL<br/><br/>In 24.1 we have added the <code>autocommit&#95;before&#95;ddl</code><a href="/docs/v24.1/session-variables#supported-variables">session variable</a>. When set to true, any schema change statement that is sent during an explicit transaction will cause the transaction to commit before executing the schema change. This setting can be used to improve compatibility with some tools that do not work well due to our limitations with schema changes in explicit transactions. It also can be used to use schema changes under <code>READ COMMITTED</code> more easily, without needing to teach the schema changer about <code>READ COMMITTED</code>.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Statistics for virtual computed columns<br/><br/>CockroachDB now collects statistics for <a href="/docs/v24.1/computed-columns#virtual-computed-columns">virtual computed columns</a>, making it possible to optimize query plans for tables that have these columns. Customers will see better query performance for queries that involve virtual computed columns.<br/><br/>For more information, you can also view a <a href="https://youtu.be/5D9jUV8Vs_U">video demo</a>.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Write Amplification Improvements<br/><br/>A number of <a href="/docs/v24.1/architecture/storage-layer">Pebble</a> improvements are now on by default, leading to a reduction in <a href="/docs/v24.1/architecture/storage-layer#inverted-lsms">write amplification</a>. Of particular note, a vast majority of range snapshots previously ingested into L0 are now ingested directly into L6 in the <a href="/docs/v24.1/architecture/storage-layer#log-structured-merge-trees">LSM</a>, reducing write and read amplification with positive effects to node stability and SQL performance.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Increased SLA for multi-region Dedicated clusters<br/><br/>CockroachDB Dedicated multi-region clusters now offer a <a href="https://www.cockroachlabs.com/cloud-terms-and-conditions/cockroachcloud-technical-service-level-agreement">five-nines (99.999%) availability target</a>.</td><td>All<sup>&#42;</sup></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Gray circle with horizontal white line (No)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b9/Eo_circle_grey_white_no-entry.svg" /></td></tr></tbody></table>

#### Change Data Capture

<table><thead><tr><th class="center-align" colspan="1" rowspan="2">Feature</th><th class="center-align" colspan="4" rowspan="1">Availability</th></tr><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Ver.</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Self-Hosted</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Dedicated</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Serverless</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td>Improved performance for changefeeds at scale<br/><br/><a href="/docs/v24.1/advanced-changefeed-configuration#mux-rangefeeds">Mux rangefeed</a> is a subsystem that improves the performance of <a href="/docs/v24.1/create-and-configure-changefeeds#enable-rangefeeds">rangefeeds</a> with scale. In v24.1, Mux rangefeeds are enabled by default.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Emit changefeed messages to an Azure Event Hub<br/><br/>Changefeeds can emit messages to an <a href="/docs/v24.1/changefeed-examples#create-a-changefeed-connected-to-an-azure-event-hubs-sink">Azure Event Hub</a>, which is compatible with Apache Kafka. You can use the Kafka changefeed and sink configuration options.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Google Cloud Pub/Sub sink for changefeeds is now generally available<br/><br/>The changefeed <a href="/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks#google-cloud-pub-sub">sink for Google Cloud Pub/Sub</a> is GA.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Filter changefeed messages based on cluster, SQL session, or row-level TTL jobs<br/><br/>Use the <code>disable&#95;changefeed&#95;replication</code> session variable to prevent changefeeds from emitting messages for any changes during that session. Also in v24.1, you can enable the <code>ignore&#95;disable&#95;changefeed&#95;replication</code> option to ignore the storage parameter or cluster setting that disables changefeed replication. These <a href="/docs/v24.1/changefeed-messages#filtering-changefeed-messages">settings</a> can be useful to manage multiple changefeed use cases on the same table.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr><tr><td>Set Kafka quotas per changefeed<br/><br/>For <a href="/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks#kafka-sink-configuration">Kafka sinks</a>, implement a resource usage limit per changefeed by setting a client ID and quota in your Kafka server's configuration.</td><td>24.1</td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td><td class="icon-center"><InlineImage alt="Green checkmark (Yes)" src="https://upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/3/3b/Eo_circle_green_checkmark.svg" /></td></tr></tbody></table>

#### Recovery

#### Migrations

<table><thead><tr><th class="center-align" colspan="1" rowspan="2">Feature</th><th class="center-align" colspan="4" rowspan="1">Availability</th></tr><tr><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Ver.</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Self-Hosted</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Dedicated</th><th colspan="1" rowspan="1">Serverless</th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td><a href="/docs/v24.1/molt/molt-fetch">MOLT Fetch</a> is GA. #### Backward-incompatible changes

Before [upgrading to CockroachDB v24.1](/docs/v24.1/upgrade-cockroach-version), be sure to review the following backward-incompatible changes, as well as [key cluster setting changes](#v24-1-0-cluster-settings), and adjust your deployment as necessary.

- [`AS OF SYSTEM TIME`](/docs/v24.1/as-of-system-time) queries can no longer use a timestamp followed by a question mark to signify a future-time value. This was an undocumented syntax. [#116830](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116830)
- The [`READ COMMITTED`](/docs/v24.1/read-committed) isolation level now requires the cluster to have a valid [enterprise license](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.1/licensing-faqs#obtain-a-license). Otherwise, transactions which are configured to run as `READ COMMITTED` will be upgraded to [`SERIALIZABLE`](/docs/v24.1/demo-serializable), as described in the next note. [#120154](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120154)
- The `sql.txn.read_committed_isolation.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) is now `true` by default. As a result for enterprise users, [`READ COMMITTED`](/docs/v24.1/read-committed) transactions are **not** automatically upgraded to [`SERIALIZABLE`](/docs/v24.1/demo-serializable), and will run as `READ COMMITTED` by default. On v23.2, refer to the [Upgrades of SQL Transaction Isolation Level](/docs/v24.1/ui-sql-dashboard#upgrades-of-sql-transaction-isolation-level) graph in the DB Console to check whether any transaction is being upgraded from a weaker isolation level to `SERIALIZABLE`, and could therefore run differently on v24.1. [#118479](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118479)

#### Features that require upgrade finalization

During a major-version upgrade, certain features and performance improvements may not be available until the upgrade is finalized.

- [Splits](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.1/architecture/distribution-layer#range-splits) no longer hold [latches](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/architecture/distribution-layer.#latch-manager) for time proportional to the range size while computing [MVCC](https://cockroachlabs.com/docs/v24.1/architecture/storage-layer#mvcc) statistics. Instead, MVCC statistics are pre-computed before the critical section of the split. As a side effect, the resulting statistics are no longer 100% accurate because they may correctly distribute writes concurrent with the split. To mitigate against this potential inaccuracy, and to prevent the statistics from drifting after successive splits, the existing stored statistics are re-computed and corrected if needed during the non-critical section of the split. [#119894](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119894)

#### Key Cluster Setting Changes

The following changes should be reviewed prior to upgrading. Default cluster settings will be used unless you have manually set a value for a setting. This can be confirmed by checking the `system.settings` table (`select * from system.settings`) to view the non-default settings.

- `sql.txn.read_committed_isolation.enabled` is now `true` by default. When set to `true`, transactions use the `READ COMMITTED` isolation level if specified by `BEGIN` / `SET` commands.
    - If the cluster setting is `false`, as was the default in v23.2, such `READ COMMITTED` transactions will instead run as `SERIALIZABLE`.
    - To check whether any transactions are being upgraded to `SERIALIZABLE`, see the [**Upgrades of SQL Transaction Isolation Level**](/docs/v24.1/ui-sql-dashboard#upgrades-of-sql-transaction-isolation-level) graph in the DB Console."
- The `changefeed.balance_range_distribution.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) is now deprecated. Instead, use the new cluster setting `changefeed.default_range_distribution_strategy`. `changefeed.default_range_distribution_strategy='balanced_simple'` has the same effect as setting `changefeed.balance_range_distribution.enabled=true`. It does not require `initial_scan='only'`, which was required by the old setting. [#115166](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115166)
- Added the [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `security.client_cert.subject_required.enabled` which enforces a mandatory requirement for the client certificate's role subject to be set. The subject can be defined through either the subject role option or by specifying the `root-cert-distinguished-name` and `node-cert-distinguished-name` properties. This setting applies to both RPC access and login via authCert. [#122368](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122368)
- The [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `sql.contention.record_serialization_conflicts.enabled` is now `on` by default. As a result, any [`40001` error](/docs/v24.1/transaction-retry-error-reference) that contains conflicting transaction information will be recorded by the contention registry, improving the ability to troubleshoot. For more information, refer to the [Insights page](/docs/v24.1/ui-insights-page) documentation. [#116664](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116664)
- The new [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `storage.sstable.compression_algorithm` configures the compression algorithm used when compressing sstable blocks. Supported values are: "snappy" and "zstd" [snappy = `1`, zstd = `2` ]. Changing the default of snappy to zstd can result in substantial performance improvement, however, the effects this change may be highly dependent on the workload and data, so experimentation is recommended before enabling zstd in production environments.
- The new setting `storage.wal_failover.unhealthy_op_threshold` allows you to set the latency threshold at which a WAL (Write-Ahead Logging) write is considered unhealthy. When exceeded, the node will attempt to write WAL entries to a secondary store's volume. For more information, refer to [#120509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120509)
- The new `server.max_open_transactions_per_gateway` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings), when set to a non-negative value, allows only admin users to execute a query if the number of open transactions on the current gateway node is already at the configured limit. [#118781](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118781)
- The new `server.redact_sensitive_settings.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) ( `false` by default), when set to `true`, redacts the values of the following settings in the output of `SHOW` commands or other introspection interfaces. In the future, newly-added sensitive cluster settings will be redacted as well. Users with the `MODIFYCLUSTERSETTING` [privilege](/docs/v24.1/security-reference/authorization#managing-privileges) can always view the unredacted settings. [#117729](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117729)
- The new boolean changefeed option [`ignore_disable_changefeed_replication`](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed#ignore-disable-changefeed-replication), when set to `true`, prevents the changefeed from filtering events even if CDC filtering is configured via the `disable_changefeed_replication` [session variable](/docs/v24.1/session-variables), `sql.ttl.changefeed_replication.disabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings), or the `ttl_disable_changefeed_replication` [table storage parameter](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#table-storage-parameters). [#120255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120255)
- The provisioned-rate field, if specified, should no longer accept a disk-name or an optional bandwidth field. To use the disk bandwidth constraint the store-spec must contain `provisioned-rate=bandwidth=<bandwidth-bytes/s>`, otherwise the cluster setting `kvadmission.store.provisioned_bandwidth` will be used. When set to a non-zero value, this is used as the provisioned bandwidth (in bytes/s), for each store. It can be overridden on a per-store basis using the --store flag. Note that setting the provisioned bandwidth to a positive value may enable disk bandwidth based admission control, since `admission.disk_bandwidth_tokens.elastic.enabled` defaults to `true`.
- Removed in v24.1:
    - `sql.show_ranges_deprecated_behavior.enabled`
    - `sql.trace.session_eventlog.enabled`
    - `changefeed.balance_range_distribution.enabled`

#### Deprecations

- `changefeed.balance_range_distribution.enable` is now deprecated. Instead, use the new [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `changefeed.default_range_distribution_strategy`. `changefeed.default_range_distribution_strategy='balanced_simple'` has the same effect as setting `changefeed.balance_range_distribution.enable=true`. It does not require `initial_scan='only'`, which was required by the old setting. [#115166](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115166)
- The `cockroach connect` command has been removed. This command was [deprecated](/docs/releases/v23.2#v23-2-0-deprecations) in CockroachDB v23.2. [#113893](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/113893)

#### Known limitations

For information about new and unresolved limitations in CockroachDB v24.1, with suggested workarounds where applicable, refer to [Known Limitations](/docs/v24.1/known-limitations).

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-rc.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0-rc.2 on Github, visit [v24.1.0-rc.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0-rc.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0-rc.1...v24.1.0-rc.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0-rc.1...v24.1.0-rc.2)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that was present since v22.2 where [changefeeds](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) with long-running [initial scans](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed#initial-scan) might incorrectly restore checkpoint job progress and drop events during [changefeed restarts](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-messages#duplicate-messages) due to transient errors or node restarts. The bug was most likely to occur in clusters with the following contributing factors:
    - The `changefeed.shutdown_checkpoint.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) was enabled (in clusters running v23.2 and later).
    - The cluster settings `changefeed.frontier_checkpoint_frequency` and `low changefeed.frontier_highwater_lag_checkpoint_threshold` were set low, which resulted in the initial scan taking many multiples of the configured frequency to complete.
    - There were multiple target tables with significant differences in row counts in one changefeed.
    - The changefeed target tables were large with many ranges.
    - The initial scan took a long time to complete (an hour or longer). [#123968](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123968)
- Fixed a crash introduced in v24.1.0-beta.2 that could occur when planning [statistics collection](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer#table-statistics) on a table with a [virtual computed column](/docs/v24.1/computed-columns) using a user-defined type and the `sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) is set to `true`. `sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled` was introduced in v24.1.0-alpha.1 as `true` by default and introduced in v23.2.5 as `false` by default. [#124064](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/124064)

### Contributors

This release includes 3 merged PRs by 3 authors.
