### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-rc.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0-rc.1 on Github, visit [v24.1.0-rc.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0-rc.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0-beta.3...v24.1.0-rc.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0-beta.3...v24.1.0-rc.1)

### SQL language changes

- Added a new [session setting](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) `optimizer_use_improved_multi_column_selectivity_estimate`, which if enabled, causes the [optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) to use an improved selectivity estimate for multi-column predicates. This setting will default to `true` on v24.2 and later, and `false` on earlier versions. [#123106](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123106)

### Operational changes

- Added two new [metrics](/docs/v24.1/metrics): `range.snapshots.upreplication.rcvd-bytes` counts the number of [Raft](/docs/v24.1/architecture/replication-layer#raft) recovery snapshot bytes received, and `range.snapshots.upreplication.sent-bytes` counts the number of Raft recovery snapshot bytes sent. Also updated `range.snapshots.recovery.rcvd-bytes` and `range.snapshots.recovery.sent-bytes` to only include Raft snapshots. A new line was added to the [**Snapshot Data Received**](/docs/v24.1/ui-replication-dashboard#snapshot-data-received) graph. [#123055](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123055)

### DB Console changes

- Added a **Replication Lag** graph to the [**Physical Cluster Replication**](/docs/v24.1/physical-cluster-replication-monitoring) dashboard to measure replication lag between primary and standby clusters using [physical cluster replication](/docs/v24.1/physical-cluster-replication-overview). [#123285](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123285)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that caused the [**Tables**](/docs/v24.1/ui-databases-page#tables-view) and [**Table Details**](/docs/v24.1/ui-databases-page#table-details) pages in the DB Console to display an incorrect value for **Table Stats Last Updated**. [#122816](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122816)
- Fixed a bug in the DB Console's [**Custom Chart**](/docs/v24.1/ui-custom-chart-debug-page) tool where store-level metrics were displayed only for the first store ID associated with the node. Now data is displayed for all stores present on a node, and a single time series is shown for each store, rather than an aggregated value for all of the node's stores. This allows finer-grained monitoring of store-level metrics. [#122705](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122705)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v22.2 that could cause the internal error `attempting to append refresh spans after the tracked timestamp has moved forward` in some edge cases. [#123136](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123136)
- Fixed a bug where a `TYPEDESC SCHEMA CHANGE` job could retry forever if the descriptor it targeted was already dropped. [#123273](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123273)
- Fixed a bug where, if the legacy schema changer was enabled, the [`CREATE SEQUENCE`](/docs/v24.1/create-sequence) command would incorrectly require the user to have the `CREATE` [privilege](/docs/v24.1/security-reference/authorization#privileges) on the parent database rather than only on the parent schema. [#123289](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123289)
- Fixed a bug where a [job](/docs/v24.1/show-jobs) would fail if it reported an out-of-bound progress fraction. The error is now logged and no longer causes the job to fail. [#122965](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122965)

### Performance improvements

- Added a new [session setting](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) `optimizer_use_improved_zigzag_join_costing`. When enabled and when the [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `enable_zigzag_join` is also enabled, the cost of zigzag joins is updated such that a zigzag join will be chosen over a scan only if it produces fewer rows than a scan. [#123106](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123106)
- Improved the selectivity estimation of multi-column filters when the multi-column distinct count is high. This prevents the [optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) from choosing a bad query plan due to over-estimating the selectivity of a multi-column predicate. [#123106](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123106)
- Improved the efficiency of error handling in the [vectorized execution engine](/docs/v24.1/vectorized-execution), to reduce the CPU overhead of statement timeout handling and reduce the potential for more statement timeouts. [#123501](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123501)
- Disabled a poorly-performing [changefeed](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) optimization that was intended to reduce duplicates during aggregator restarts. [#123597](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123597)

### Contributors

This release includes 57 merged PRs by 24 authors.

Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>

#### Full CockroachDB executable

<LinkedPageTabs
  currentPath="/docs/releases/v24.1"
  items={[
    {
      title: "Linux Intel",
      href: "https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.1.0-beta.3.linux-amd64.tgz",
    },
    {
      title: "Linux ARM",
      href: "https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.1.0-beta.3.linux-arm64.tgz",
    },
    {
      title: "Mac Intel (Experimental)",
      href: "https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.1.0-beta.3.darwin-10.9-amd64.tgz",
    },
    {
      title: "Mac ARM (Experimental)",
      href: "https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.1.0-beta.3.darwin-11.0-arm64.tgz",
    },
    {
      title: "Windows (Experimental)",
      href: "https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-v24.1.0-beta.3.windows-6.2-amd64.zip",

#### SQL-only command-line client executable

<LinkedPageTabs
  currentPath="/docs/releases/v24.1"
  items={[
    {
      title: "Linux Intel",
      href: "https://binaries.cockroachdb.com/cockroach-sql-v24.1.0-beta.3.linux-amd64.tgz",

<Tabs>
<Tab title="Windows (Experimental)">

<Warning>
CockroachDB executable for Windows is experimental and not suitable for production deployments. Windows 8 or higher is required.
</Warning>

</Tab>
</Tabs>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-beta.3
```

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0-beta.2...v24.1.0-beta.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0-beta.2...v24.1.0-beta.3)

### SQL language changes

- Updated the [`SHOW GRANTS`](/docs/v24.1/show-grants) responses to display the `object_type` and `object_name`, which has replaced the `relation_name` column. [#122823](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122823)
- Added [external connection](/docs/v24.1/create-external-connection) granted privileges to the [`SHOW GRANTS`](/docs/v24.1/show-grants) command. [#122823](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122823)
- Introduced three new [cluster settings](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) for controlling table statistics forecasting:
    - [`sql.stats.forecasts.min_observations`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) is the minimum number of observed statistics required to produce a forecast.
    - [`sql.stats.forecasts.min_goodness_of_fit`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) is the minimum R² (goodness of fit) measurement required from all predictive models to use a forecast.
    - [`sql.stats.forecasts.max_decrease`](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) is the most a prediction can decrease, expressed as the minimum ratio of the prediction to the lowest prior observation. [#122459](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122459)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that could lead to descriptors having privileges to roles that no longer exist. Added an automated clean up for [dropped roles](/docs/v24.1/drop-role) inside descriptors. [#122701](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122701)
- Fixed a bug where [client certificate authentication](/docs/v24.1/authentication#client-authentication) combined with [identity maps](/docs/v24.1/sso-sql#identity-map-configuration) ( `server.identity_map.configuration` ) did not work since v23.1. For the feature to work correctly, the client must specify a valid db user in the [connection string](/docs/v24.1/connection-parameters). [#122738](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122738)
- Fixed a bug where the [row-based execution engine](/docs/v24.1/architecture/sql-layer#query-execution) could drop a [`LIMIT`](/docs/v24.1/limit-offset) clause when there was an [`ORDER BY`](/docs/v24.1/order-by) clause, and the ordering was partially provided by an input operator. For example, this bug could occur with an ordering such as `ORDER BY a, b` when the scanned index was only ordered on column `a`. The impact of this bug was that more rows may have been returned than specified by the `LIMIT` clause. This bug is only present when not using the [vectorized execution engine](/docs/v24.1/architecture/sql-layer#vectorized-query-execution). That is, when running with `SET vectorize = off;`. This bug has existed since CockroachDB v22.1. [#122837](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122837)
- Previously, CockroachDB could run into an internal error when evaluating [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) routines with nested blocks. The bug is only present in 24.1.0-beta versions. This bug is now fixed. [#122939](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122939)
- Fixed a bug where [`UPDATE`](/docs/v24.1/update) and [`UPSERT`](/docs/v24.1/upsert) queries with a subquery were sometimes inappropriately using implicit [`FOR UPDATE`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update) locking within the subquery. This bug has existed since implicit `FOR UPDATE` locking was introduced in v20.1. [#121391](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121391)
- [Dropping](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#drop-column) and [adding](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#add-column) a column with the same name no longer results in a `"column already exists error"`. [#122631](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122631)
- Fixed a bug that could cause an internal error of the form `invalid datum type given:..., expected...` when a `RECORD` -returning [user-defined function](/docs/v24.1/user-defined-functions), used as a data source, was supplied a column definition list with mismatched types. This bug has existed since v23.1. [#122305](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122305)
- Fixed a bug that could result in an internal error when attempting to create a [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) routine using the (unsupported) `%ROWTYPE` syntax for a variable declaration. Now, an expected syntax error is returned instead. [#122966](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122966)
- Fixed a bug that could result in an assertion error during evaluation of [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) routines that invoke procedures while using `DEFAULT` arguments. The bug was present in v24.1.0-beta releases and is now fixed. [#122943](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122943)
- Previously, privileges granted for [external connections](/docs/v24.1/create-external-connection) were displaying in `SHOW SYSTEM GRANTS` with no associated object name. Now these privileges are no longer displayed. Instead, the statement `SHOW GRANTS ON EXTERNAL CONNECTION` should be used to view external connection privileges with their associated object name. [#122857](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122857)
- Statistics forecasts of zero rows can cause suboptimal [query plans](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer). Forecasting will now avoid predicting zero rows for most downward-trending statistics. [#122459](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122459)
- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2 that could cause a [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) variable assignment to not be executed if the variable was never referenced after the assignment. [#123045](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123045)

### Performance improvements

- More efficient [query plans](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) are now generated for queries with text similarity filters, for example, `text_col % 'foobar'`. These plans are generated if the `optimizer_use_trigram_similarity_optimization` [session setting](/docs/v24.1/set-vars) is enabled. It is disabled by default. [#122838](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122838)
- The [optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) now costs `distinct-on` operators more accurately. It may produce more efficient query plans in some cases. [#122850](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122850)
- Improved the speed for optimization of some statements using `GROUP BY` or `DISTINCT` or `ON CONFLICT` by skipping the [optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) rule `SplitGroupByScanIntoUnionScans` when it is not needed. [#123034](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/123034)

### Contributors

This release includes 56 merged PRs by 25 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-beta.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0-beta.2 on Github, visit [v24.1.0-beta.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0-beta.2).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0-beta.1...v24.1.0-beta.2](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0-beta.1...v24.1.0-beta.2)

### Security updates

- Added the [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `security.client_cert.subject_required.enabled` that enforces a mandatory requirement for the client certificate's role subject to be set. The subject can be defined through either the subject role option or by specifying the `root-cert-distinguished-name` and `node-cert-distinguished-name` properties. This setting applies to both RPC access and login via authCert. [#122368](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122368)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug where table statistics were sometimes not collected on tables that have virtual [computed columns](/docs/v24.1/computed-columns) of a user-defined type when the `sql.stats.virtual_computed_columns.enabled` cluster setting is enabled. The setting was introduced in v23.2.4 and is disabled by default. Only clusters running v23.2.4 with the non-default setting are affected. [#122320](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122320)

### Contributors

This release includes 52 merged PRs by 28 authors.

</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-beta.1
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0-beta.1 on Github, visit [v24.1.0-beta.1 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0-beta.1).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0-alpha.5...v24.1.0-beta.1](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0-alpha.5...v24.1.0-beta.1)

### SQL language changes

- [`SHOW JOBS`](/docs/v24.1/show-jobs) no longer displays some internal retry counter columns ( `last_run`, `next_run`, `num_runs` ) and now only shows the `statement`, `trace_id`, and `execution_errors` columns when inspecting a specific job ID or IDs. [#121286](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121286)
- [`SHOW JOBS`](/docs/v24.1/show-jobs) now shortens long job descriptions to 100 characters to make the table easier to read while the full description and statement can be inspected using `SHOW JOB` or `SHOW JOBS` on specific job IDs. [#121286](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121286)
- Extended [`pg_depend`](/docs/v24.1/pg-catalog) to include dependencies between UDFs. [#121313](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121313)
- With [`sql_safe_updates`](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) set to `true`, [`SELECT FOR UPDATE` and `SELECT FOR SHARE`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update) statements now return an error if they do not contain either a `WHERE` clause or a `LIMIT` clause. Also, `UPDATE` and `DELETE` statements without `WHERE` clauses but with `LIMIT` clauses now bypass `sql_safe_updates`, which better matches MySQL behavior. [#121466](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121466)
- Added support for [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) `CALL` statements. It is now possible to call a stored procedure from a PL/pgSQL routine. [#121743](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121743)
- `DEFAULT` expressions for input parameters of [user-defined functions](/docs/v24.1/user-defined-functions) and stored procedures are now supported. [#121811](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121811)

### Command-line changes

- The [`--enterprise-encryption`](/docs/v24.1/encryption#starting-a-node-with-encryption) flag now accepts the special value `path=*` to apply the specified keys to all stores. [#121111](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121111)

### DB Console changes

- The **Commit Latency** chart in the [**Changefeeds** dashboard](/docs/v24.1/ui-cdc-dashboard) now aggregates by max instead of by sum for multi-node [changefeeds](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview). This more accurately reflects the amount of time for events to be acknowledged by the downstream sink. [#120787](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120787)
- Introduced a license expiration message in the [DB Console](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview) in the top-right corner of the primary header. This message indicates the remaining days before license expiration for clusters with an Enterprise or trial license. [#120830](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120830)
- The [**Jobs** table](/docs/v24.1/ui-jobs-page#jobs-table) page no longer includes two columns related to a deprecated internal implementation detail (last execution time and execution count). [#121286](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121286)
- The timeseries graphs shown on the [**SQL Activity**](/docs/v24.1/ui-overview#sql-activity) statement details page in the DB Console will now render properly, after fixing a bug related to setting the time range of the charts. [#121461](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121461)
- [Index recommendations](/docs/v24.1/ui-databases-page#index-recommendations) in the DB Console will now function properly for indexes on tables or columns whose names contain quotation marks or whitespace. For example: `CREATE INDEX ON "my table" ("my col");`. [#122120](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122120)

### Bug fixes

- Sequence options for `NO MINVALUE` and `NO MAXVALUE` now match PostgreSQL behavior. Sequence `MINVALUE` and `MAXVALUE` automatically adjust to new types bounds mirroring behavior of PostgreSQL. [#121310](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121310)
- CockroachDB could previously "leak" reported memory usage as accounted by the internal memory accounting system, the limit for which is configured with the `--max-sql-memory` flag, on long-running sessions that issue many (hundreds of thousands or more) transactions. This, in turn, could result in `"root: memory budget exceeded"` errors for other queries. This bug was present in versions v23.1.17 and v23.2.3 and is now fixed. [#121873](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121873)
- CockroachDB could previously incorrectly evaluate `IN` expressions that had `INT2` or `INT4` type on the left side and values outside of the range of the left side on the right side. The bug has been present since at least v21.1 and is now fixed. [#121954](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121954)
- Fixed a slow memory leak in the deprecated [Pub/Sub changefeeds](/docs/v24.1/changefeed-sinks), which can accumulate when restarting or canceling many deprecated Pub/Sub changefeeds. The bug had been present since the deprecated Pub/Sub changefeed was introduced in a testing release of v22.1. [#121867](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121867)

### Contributors

This release includes 134 merged PRs by 36 authors.

## v24.1.0-alpha.5

Release Date: April 1, 2024

</Warning>

</Note>

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-alpha.5
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0-alpha.5 on Github, visit [v24.1.0-alpha.5 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0-alpha.5).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0-alpha.4...v24.1.0-alpha.5](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0-alpha.4...v24.1.0-alpha.5)

### Enterprise edition changes

- [Changefeeds](/docs/v24.1/change-data-capture-overview) now default to evenly distributing their work across all replicas, including followers, regardless of leaseholder placement. On upgrade to v24.1, running changefeed jobs will be restarted automatically as part of the upgrade process and will default to distributing work across replicas. To disable this behavior, set the [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `changefeed.random_replica_selection.enabled` to `false`. If disabled, changefeed planning reverts to its previous behavior for distributing work. [#120077](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120077)
- When [physical cluster replication](/docs/v24.1/physical-cluster-replication-overview) is enabled, the output of the `SHOW VIRTUAL CLUSTER... WITH REPLICATION STATUS` command now displays replication lag. [#120782](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120782)
- When [physical cluster replication](/docs/v24.1/physical-cluster-replication-overview) is enabled, the output of the `SHOW VIRTUAL CLUSTER WITH REPLICATION STATUS to 1` command has changed:
    - The output no longer displays `replication_job_id` or `service_mode` return fields.
    - The `data_state` field has been renamed to `status`.
    - The fields that are displayed are now ordered as follows: `retained_time`, `replicated_time`, `replication_lag`, `cutover_time`, `status`. [#120782](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120782)
- You can now run [physical cluster replication](/docs/v24.1/physical-cluster-replication-overview) from an [existing CockroachDB cluster](/docs/v24.1/set-up-physical-cluster-replication#set-up-pcr-from-an-existing-cluster), without [cluster virtualization](/docs/v24.1/cluster-virtualization-overview) enabled, to a standby cluster with cluster virtualization enabled. [#122001](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/122001)

### SQL language changes

- You can now specify a condition for the [PL/pgSQL statements](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) `EXIT` and `CONTINUE`. [#120686](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120686)
- A [stored procedure](/docs/v24.1/stored-procedures) can now invoke another stored procedure using a [`CALL` statement](/docs/v24.1/call). [#120674](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120674)
- You can now use a [`SET TRANSACTION`](/docs/v24.1/set-transaction) statement within a [PL/pgSQL stored procedure](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) to configure the transaction isolation level, timestamp, or priority, or to set the transaction to read-only. A `SET TRANSACTION` statement must immediately follow a `COMMIT` or `ROLLBACK`, with no other statements or block boundaries between them. [#120456](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120456)
- The new [session variable](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) `optimizer_use_virtual_computed_column_stats`, when enabled, configures the [cost-based optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) to use [table statistics](/docs/v24.1/show-statistics) on virtual computed columns. [#120668](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120668)
- An [identity column](/docs/v24.1/create-table#identity-columns) can now drop the `IDENTITY` constraint and related sequence using the following SQL statement:

    ```sql
    ALTER TABLE {table_name} ALTER COLUMN {column_name} DROP IDENTITY [IF EXISTS];
    ```

    `IF EXISTS` is optional, and skips the command if the column is not an identity column. [#119263](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119263)
- A shared lock that is acquired explicitly using [`SELECT FOR SHARE`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update) or implicitly by a [read-committed transaction](/docs/v24.1/read-committed), can now be re-acquired with higher strength by either using a [`SELECT FOR UPDATE`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update) statement or by writing to the key. [#119671](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119671)
- [Stored procedures](/docs/v24.1/stored-procedures) now support `OUT` and `INOUT` parameter classes. [#120851](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120851)
- The [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) `EXIT` and `CONTINUE` statements can now use labels to specify which loop or block is the target. [#120733](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120733)

### Operational changes

- You can now enable asynchronous buffering of `file-group` [log sinks](/docs/v24.1/configure-logs) using the `buffering` [configuration options](/docs/v24.1/configure-logs#log-buffering-for-network-sinks) either by default or to an individual `file-group`. The `buffering` configuration option is incompatible with the `buffered-writes` configuration option. To try the `buffering` option, you must set `buffered-writes: false`. Cockroach Labs recommends setting `max-staleness` to `1s` and `flush-trigger-size` to `256KiB`. [#120428](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120428)
- A minimum [Raft scheduler](/docs/v24.1/architecture/replication-layer#raft) concurrency is now enforced per store so that nodes with many stores do not spread workers too thin. This helps to avoid high scheduler latency across replicas on a store when load is imbalanced. [#120162](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120162)
- The new [metrics](/docs/v24.1/metrics) `kv.split.estimated_stats` and `kv.split.total_bytes_estimates` track the number of splits that produce [MVCC](/docs/v24.1/architecture/storage-layer#mvcc) statistic estimates and the total bytes of estimates produced. [#119894](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119894)
- The new [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `storage.sstable.compression_algorithm` configures the compression algorithm used when compressing sstable blocks. [#120784](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120784)
- The new [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `kv.dist_sender.proxy.enabled`, which is enabled by default, causes proxy requests to be routed through a follower replica when the leaseholder is unavailable. [#117340](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/117340)
- The new startup flag `--wal-failover` allows you to explicitly set the path for WAL failover of a single-store node. [#120783](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120783)
- Cluster virtualization is now enabled using either of the new startup flags `--virtualized` or `--virtualized-empty` instead of the `--config-profile` flag. [#120813](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120813)
- The following metrics, which track the SQL statistics subsystem's task to flush in-memory statistics to persisted storage, are now more consistent with other metrics used in the subsystem.
    - `sql.stats.flushes.successful`: Number of times SQL statistics have been flushed successfully to persistent storage.
    - `sql.stats.flushes.failed`: Number of attempted SQL statistics flushes that failed with errors.
    - `sql.stats.flush.latency`: The latency of attempted SQL statistics flushes to persistent storage, including both successes and failures. [#120709](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120709)
- The following new [metrics](/docs/v24.1/metrics) track the number and outcome of proxy requests when `kv.dist_sender.proxy.enabled` is set to `true`:
    - `distsender.rpc.proxy.sent`
    - `distsender.rpc.proxy.err`
    - `distsender.rpc.proxy.forward.sent`
    - `distsender.rpc.proxy.forward.err`

        Cockroach Labs recommends monitoring and alerting on `distsender.rpc.proxy.sent`, because it indicates a possible network partition. [#120239](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120239)
- The `provisioned-rate` field of a node's store specification can no longer be used to add constraints for the disk name or bandwidth. By default, bandwidth is constrained according to the [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `kv.store.admission.provisioned_bandwidth`. To override this setting for a specific node, the storage specification must contain `provisioned-rate=bandwidth={bandwidth-bytes/s}`. [#120895](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120895)
- Removal of the [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) `kv.rangefeed.scheduler.enabled`, which was announced in [v24.1.0-alpha.1](/docs/releases/v24.1#v24-1-0-alpha-1), has been reverted, and the cluster setting is reinstated. [#121164](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121164)

### DB Console changes

- In generated statement fingerprints in the DB Console [**Statements** page](/docs/v24.1/ui-statements-page), lists with only literals or placeholders or similar subexpressions are shortened to their first item followed by " **more** ". [#120507](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120507)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug introduced in v23.2 that could cause a [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) routine to return incorrect results when the routine included:
    1. At least one parameter.
    2. An `IF` statement with one leak-proof branch and one branch with side effects. [#120451](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120451)
- Fixed a rare bug where a `BACKUP` command issued shortly after an [`ALTER TABLE {table_name} SET (exclude_data_from_backup = true)`](/docs/v24.1/take-full-and-incremental-backups#exclude-a-tables-data-from-backups) could exclude data from an unrelated table from the backup. [#120188](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120188)
- Fixed a behavior where a memory exhaustion error during a schema change was treated as a permanent failure and reverted. Such schema changes are now retried instead of reverted. [#120806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120806)
- Fixed a bug where the `attname` for a dropped column was not correctly padded with 8 `.` characters to be compatible with PostgreSQL. [#120861](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120861)

### Performance improvements

- Splits no longer hold latches for time proportional to the range size while computing MVCC statistics. Instead, MVCC statistics are pre-computed before the critical section of the split. As a side effect, the resulting statistics are no longer 100% accurate because they may correctly distribute writes concurrent with the split. To mitigate against this potential inaccuracy, and to prevent the statistics from drifting after successive splits, the existing stored statistics are re-computed and corrected if needed during the non-critical section of the split. [#119894](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119894)
- The [cost-based optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) now generates more efficient query plans for some queries with `OFFSET` clauses. [#121160](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/121160)

### Contributors

This release includes 157 merged PRs by 44 authors. We would like to thank the following contributors from the CockroachDB community:

- Andrew Delph

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-alpha.4
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0-alpha.4 on Github, visit [v24.1.0-alpha.4 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0-alpha.4).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0-alpha.3...v24.1.0-alpha.4](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0-alpha.3...v24.1.0-alpha.4)

### Security updates

- When [configuring logs](/docs/v24.1/configure-logs#output-to-files), `file-permissions` are now applied literally, such that `file-permissions: 644` will result in files with permissions matching `644` (instead of the previous behavior's `640` ). Previously, CockroachDB's `umask` (which is always at least `007` ) was being applied after the `file-permissions` field was used to create files, meaning the resulting permissions did not match those specified in the log configuration. [#120669](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120669)

### General changes

- The following [metrics](/docs/v24.1/metrics) were added for observability of per-store disk events:
    - `storage.disk.read.count`
    - `storage.disk.read.bytes`
    - `storage.disk.read.time`
    - `storage.disk.write.count`
    - `storage.disk.write.bytes`
    - `storage.disk.write.time`
    - `storage.disk.io.time`
    - `storage.disk.weightedio.time`
    - `storage.disk.iopsinprogress`

        The metrics match the definitions of the `sys.host.disk.*` system metrics. [#119885](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119885)

### Enterprise edition changes

- `server.controller.default_target_cluster` can now be set to any virtual cluster name by default, including a virtual cluster yet to be created or have service started. [#120080](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120080)
- The [`READ COMMITTED`](/docs/v24.1/read-committed) isolation level now requires the cluster to have a valid enterprise license. [#120154](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120154)
- The new boolean changefeed option [`ignore_disable_changefeed_replication`](/docs/v24.1/create-changefeed#ignore-disable-changefeed-replication), when set to `true`, prevents the changefeed from filtering events even if CDC filtering is configured via the `disable_changefeed_replication` [session variable](/docs/v24.1/session-variables), `sql.ttl.changefeed_replication.disabled` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings), or the `ttl_disable_changefeed_replication` [table storage parameter](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#table-storage-parameters). [#120255](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120255)

### SQL language changes

- Added support for the [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) `COMMIT` and `ROLLBACK` statements. [#119647](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119647)
- [Identity columns](/docs/v24.1/create-table#identity-columns) now support enhanced sequence management through the [`ALTER [COLUMN] column_name SET sequence_option`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#alter-column) and [`ALTER [COLUMN] column_name RESTART [WITH restart]`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#alter-column) commands. This update facilitates the fine-tuning of identity column sequences. [#119432](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119432)
- It is now possible to use the `STRICT` option with [`SELECT... INTO`](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql#assign-a-result-to-a-variable) and [`RETURNING... INTO`](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql#assign-a-result-to-a-variable) in order to enforce that a SQL statement within a [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) routine returns exactly one row. [#120486](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120486)
- Added a [session setting](/docs/v24.1/session-variables) `plpgsql_use_strict_into`, which causes PL/pgSQL [`SELECT... INTO`](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql#assign-a-result-to-a-variable) and [`RETURNING... INTO`](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql#assign-a-result-to-a-variable) to require exactly one row from the SQL statement, similar to Oracle behavior. [#120486](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120486)
- Added a new `failure_count INT NOT NULL` column to `crdb_internal.node_statement_statistics`. It represents the number of recorded statement execution failures for the given statement, as a new component of the overall statistics. [#120236](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120236)
- The `FORCE_INVERTED_INDEX` hint causes the [optimizer](/docs/v24.1/cost-based-optimizer) to prefer a query plan scan over any inverted index of the hinted table. An error is emitted if no such query plan can be generated. [#120384](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120384)
- The `REPAIRCLUSTERMETADATA` privilege has been aliased to `REPAIRCLUSTER`. Both names can be used interchangeably. [#116844](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/116844)

### Operational changes

- The new [`cockroach start`](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start) option [`--wal-failover=among-stores` or `COCKROACH_WAL_FAILOVER=among-stores`](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start#write-ahead-log-wal-failover) environment variable will configure a multi-store CockroachDB node to fail over a store's write-ahead log (WAL) to another store's data directory. Failing over the write-ahead log may allow some operations against a store to continue completing, even if the underlying storage is temporarily unavailable. This feature is in [preview](/docs/v24.1/cockroachdb-feature-availability#features-in-preview). [#120509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120509)
- The new `storage.wal_failover.unhealthy_op_threshold` [cluster setting](/docs/v24.1/cluster-settings) allows configuring the latency threshold at which a WAL write is considered unhealthy. [#120509](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120509)
- Two new metrics track the status of the SQL Activity Update job, which pre-aggregates top K information within the SQL statistics subsytem and writes the results to `system.statement_activity` and `system.transaction_activity`:
    - `sql.stats.activity.updates.successful`: Number of successful updates made by the SQL activity updater job.
    - `sql.stats.activity.update.latency`: The latency of updates made by the SQL activity updater job. Includes failed update attempts. [#120522](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120522)
- Added a new counter metric, `sql.stats.flush.done_signals.ignored`, that tracks the number of times the SQL activity update job has ignored the signal that indicates that a flush has completed. This metric may indicate that the SQL activity update job is taking longer than expected to complete. [#120522](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120522)
- Added a new counter metric, `sql.stats.activity.updates.failed`, to measure the number of update attempts made by the SQL activity update job that failed with errors. [#120522](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120522)
- Added a new counter metric, `sql.stats.flush.fingerprint.count`, that tracks the number of unique statement and transaction fingerprints included in the SQL stats flush. [#120522](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120522)
- The `/_status/stores` endpoint now includes `node_id`, `dir`, and `wal_failover_path` fields to show the store's node ID, data directory, and path to the configured WAL failover secondary, if configured. [#120677](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120677)

### Command-line changes

- The new `--go-gc-percent` flag of the [`cockroach start`](/docs/v24.1/cockroach-start) command controls the garbage collection target percentage of the Go runtime, mirroring the existing `GOGC` environment variable. A garbage collection is triggered when the ratio of freshly allocated data to live data remaining after the previous collection reaches this percentage. If left unspecified and if a Go soft memory limit is configured (i.e., not explicitly disabled via `--max-go-memory` or `GOMEMLIMIT` ), the garbage collection target percentage defaults to 300%. Setting the flag to a negative value disables the target percentage garbage collection heuristic, and only the soft memory limit heuristic triggers garbage collection. To monitor the impact of this change in the DB Console, look for an increase in **Memory usage** in the [Hardware dashboard](/docs/v24.1/ui-hardware-dashboard#memory-usage) and an increase in **Go total memory usage** in the [Runtime dashboard](/docs/v24.1/ui-runtime-dashboard#memory-usage). This does not increase the risk of an out-of-memory exception (OOM), because the Go memory limit (controlled by the `--max-go-memory` flag or the `GOMEMLIMIT` environment variable) prevents Go from consuming too much memory. [#119605](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119605)

### DB Console changes

- The [**Queues** dashboard](/docs/v24.1/ui-queues-dashboard) now includes lease queue metrics. [#119386](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119386)
- The DB Console **SQL Activity** [**Statement Fingerprint**](/docs/v24.1/ui-statements-page#statement-fingerprint-page) page has replaced the **Failed?** boolean column with a **Failure Count** column that shows the number of failed executions for the given statement fingerprint. In the **SQL Activity** table, the same statement fingeprint no longer appears in separate rows for failed executions and successful executions. Instead, they are combined into a single statement fingerprint. [#120236](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120236)
- The DB Console now displays an alert message when a license has expired or will expire in fewer than 15 days. [#120490](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120490)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug with [`DROP SCHEMA... CASCADE`](/docs/v24.1/drop-schema) that could lead to dangling function references in other schemas accessing any functions. [#119932](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119932)
- Fixed a bug where a [`RESTORE`](/docs/v24.1/restore) of a backup that itself contained a table created by the `RESTORE` of a table with an in-progress [`IMPORT INTO`](/docs/v24.1/import-into) would fail to restore all rows. [#120414](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120414)
- Fixed a bug where [identity columns](/docs/v24.1/create-table#identity-columns) without any configured sequence options did not display the default values for identity attributes in `information_schema`. [#119459](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119459)
- Fixed a bug where a [`GRANT... ON ALL TABLES`](/docs/v24.1/grant) statement could fail if sequences existed and they did not support a privilege (e.g., `BACKUP` ). [#120685](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120685)
- Fixed a bug where an [`EXPLAIN (DDL)`](/docs/v24.1/explain) statement would generate event log entries for schema changes that were not executed. [#120563](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120563)

### Contributors

This release includes 153 merged PRs by 179 authors.

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-alpha.3
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0-alpha.3 on Github, visit [v24.1.0-alpha.3 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0-alpha.3).

### Changelog

View a detailed changelog on GitHub: [v24.1.0-alpha.2...v24.1.0-alpha.3](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/compare/v24.1.0-alpha.2...v24.1.0-alpha.3)

### Enterprise edition changes

- [`cockroach gen encryption-key`](/docs/v24.1/encryption) now accepts a `--version=2` parameter. Version 2 keys activate a new encryption implementation with improved performance. This is expected to become the default in CockroachDB v24.2. [#119913](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119913)

### SQL language changes

- Mutation statements such as [`UPDATE`](/docs/v24.1/update) and [`DELETE`](/docs/v24.1/delete) as well as locking statements such as [`SELECT FOR UPDATE`](/docs/v24.1/select-for-update) are not allowed in read-only transactions or [`AS OF SYSTEM TIME`](/docs/v24.1/as-of-system-time) transactions. This fixes an oversight where CockroachDB was allowing mutation statements and locking statements in implicit single-statement transactions using `AS OF SYSTEM TIME`. [#120097](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120097)
- Added support for `RETURN` statements with no expression for routines with `OUT` parameters and routines with a `VOID` return type. [#120043](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120043)
- [`ALTER COLUMN`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table#alter-column) can now change columns to an identity column by using the syntax in one of the following:

    ```sql
    ALTER TABLE t ALTER COLUMN c ADD GENERATED ALWAYS AS IDENTITY [( <opt_sequence_option_list> )]
    ALTER TABLE t ALTER COLUMN c ADD GENERATED BY DEFAULT AS IDENTITY[( <opt_sequence_option_list> )]
    ```

    Identity columns can have their identity type altered by using the syntax in one of the following statements:

    ```sql
    ALTER TABLE t ALTER COLUMN c SET GENERATED ALWAYS
    ALTER TABLE t ALTER COLUMN c SET GENERATED BY DEFAULT
    ```

    [#115889](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115889)
- Added support for the [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) `NULL` statement. [#119037](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119037)
- [`crdb_internal.leases`](/docs/v24.1/crdb-internal) is now behind the [`VIEWCLUSTERMETADATA` privilege](/docs/v24.1/security-reference/authorization#supported-privileges). [#120014](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120014)
- [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v24.1/plpgsql) blocks can now be nested in a block that has an exception handler. [#120045](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120045)

### DB Console changes

- Resolved an issue where clusters with multiple stores per node may list inaccurate region/node information in the [**Databases**](/docs/v24.1/ui-databases-page) page. [#119260](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119260)
- `VIEW` type tables will no longer display in the DB Console [**Databases**](/docs/v24.1/ui-databases-page) pages. Previously these would be listed with no information, only displaying errors. [#119890](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119890)
- Fixed an intermittent page crash in the [**Schema Insights**](/docs/v24.1/ui-insights-page#schema-insights-tab) tab. [#120137](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120137)
- Fixed a bug where the **Rows written** value was incorrectly showing the **Rows read** value on the [**Insights**](/docs/v24.1/ui-insights-page) page. [#120145](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120145)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that occurred when using [`ALTER TABLE`](/docs/v24.1/alter-table) to drop and re-add a [`CHECK` constraint](/docs/v24.1/check) with the same name. [#120008](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120008)
- Fixed a bug in which it was possible to [`SET transaction_read_only = false`](/docs/v24.1/show-vars#supported-variables) during an [`AS OF SYSTEM TIME`](/docs/v24.1/as-of-system-time) transaction. [#120097](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/120097)
- Fixed a bug that caused a slow memory leak that could accumulate when opening many new connections. The bug was present in v22.2.9+ and v23.1+ versions. [#119799](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119799)

### Contributors

This release includes 90 merged PRs by 35 authors. We would like to thank the following contributors from the CockroachDB community:

- Andrew Delph

### Docker image

[Multi-platform images](https://docs.docker.com/build/building/multi-platform) include support for both Intel and ARM. Multi-platform images do not take up additional space on your Docker host.

Within the multi-platform image, both Intel and ARM images are **generally available** for production use.

To download the Docker image:

```shell
docker pull cockroachdb/cockroach-unstable:v24.1.0-alpha.2
```

### Source tag

To view or download the source code for CockroachDB v24.1.0-alpha.2 on Github, visit [v24.1.0-alpha.2 source tag](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/releases/tag/v24.1.0-alpha.2).

### Security updates

- [DB Console](/docs/v23.2/ui-overview) `session` cookie is now marked `HttpOnly` to prevent it from being read by any JavaScript code. [#119261](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119261)
- [DB Console](/docs/v23.2/ui-overview) cookies are now marked `Secure` for the browser when the cluster is running in secure mode. [#119261](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119261)

### General changes

- [Gateways](/docs/v23.2/architecture/life-of-a-distributed-transaction#gateway) will now detect faulty or stalled [replicas](/docs/v23.2/architecture/overview#architecture-replica) and use other replicas instead, which can prevent them getting stuck in certain cases (e.g., with [disk stalls](/docs/v23.2/cluster-setup-troubleshooting#disk-stalls) ). This behavior can be disabled via the [cluster setting](/docs/v23.2/cluster-settings) `kv.dist_sender.circuit_breaker.enabled`. [#118943](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118943)

### Enterprise edition changes

- Added a new [`ALTER ROLE... SUBJECT` option](/docs/v24.1/alter-role#set-the-subject-role-option-for-certificate-based-authentication). This role option can be set to a subject distinguished name in [RFC 2253](https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc2253) or [RFC 4514](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc4514) format. If set, then during client certificate authentication, certs that do not match the configured distinguished name will be rejected. [#119135](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119135)
- [Changefeeds](/docs/v23.2/create-changefeed) support a new scheme `azure-event-hub://` for Kafka data streaming to Azure event hubs. The `sinkURL` must include mandatory parameters `shared_access_key_name` and `shared_access_key`. By default and as required, the options `tls_enabled=true`, `sasl_handshake=true`, `sasl_enabled=true`, and `sasl_mechanism=PLAIN` are applied, as they are the only supported options. Other parameters such as `topic_name` and `topic_prefix` are also supported. An example URI is: `azure-event-hub://myeventhubs.servicebus.windows.net:9093?shared_access_key_name=abc&shared_access_key=123`. [#115806](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/115806)

### SQL language changes

- Added an option for node-level [sequence](/docs/v23.2/serial) caching. All the sessions on the node can share the same cache, which can be concurrently accessed. The `serial_normalization` [session variable](/docs/v23.2/set-vars#supported-variables) can now be set to the value `sql_sequence_cached_node`. If this value is set, the [cluster setting](/docs/v23.2/cluster-settings) `sql.defaults.serial_sequences_cache_size` can be used to control the number of values to cache in a node, with a default of 256. The `PER NODE CACHE` sequence option (syntax is `[ [ PER NODE ] CACHE # ]` ) is now fully implemented and will allow nodes to cache sequence numbers. A cache size of 1 means there is no cache, and cache sizes of less than 1 are not valid. [#118546](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/118546)

### Bug fixes

- Fixed a bug that prevented the use of [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v23.2/plpgsql) routines with complex variable names that require double quotes. This bug had existed since v23.2. [#119034](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119034)
- Fixed a bug that could cause creation of a syntactically invalid [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v23.2/plpgsql) routine to return the wrong error. This bug had existed since v23.2. [#119034](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119034)
- Fixed a bug that could result in a syntax error if a [PL/pgSQL](/docs/v23.2/plpgsql) routine was created with an escaped string constant in the routine body. This bug had existed since v23.2. [#119034](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119034)
- Fixed a bug where running a [changefeed](/docs/v23.2/change-data-capture-overview) that targets a table with a user-defined type column and with the [`envelope` option](/docs/v23.2/create-changefeed#envelope) set to any value other than `wrapped` would cause a node panic due to a nil dereference. [#119639](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119639)
- Fixed a bug where running [`RESTORE`](/docs/v23.2/restore) on certain backups would open a very large number of connections to the backup storage provider. [#119840](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119840)
- Previously, a user with the `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` [privilege](/docs/v23.2/security-reference/authorization#managing-privileges) could see constants inside of queries that originated from other [users](/docs/v23.2/security-reference/authorization#roles) in the [`SHOW SESSIONS`](/docs/v23.2/show-sessions) output. This information is now properly redacted. [#119820](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119820)
- Previously, the [`SHOW QUERIES`](/docs/v23.2/show-statements) and [`SHOW STATEMENTS`](/docs/v23.2/show-statements) commands incorrectly required the user to have the `VIEWACTIVITY` or `VIEWACTIVITYREDACTED` [privilege](/docs/v23.2/security-reference/authorization#managing-privileges). This is now fixed, as a user should always be able to view their own queries, even without this privilege. [#119820](https://github.com/cockroachdb/cockroach/pull/119820)

### Contributors

This release includes 1939 merged PRs by 109 authors.

## v24.1.0-alpha.1

Release Date: March 7, 2024

### Downloads

<Warning>
CockroachDB v24.1.0-alpha.1 is a testing release. Testing releases are intended for testing and experimentation only, and are not qualified for production environments and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments.
</Warning>

<Note>
Experimental downloads are not qualified for production use and not eligible for support or uptime SLA commitments, whether they are for testing releases or production releases.
</Note>
